Sole active sourcing list for the Social Sciences Wiki. Prioritized, tiered.
Update on every ingest: mark completed items, revise notes, add new priorities
as gaps become visible.

**Status:** Active — 11+ sources ingested (Comte, Tocqueville, Veblen, Durkheim *Suicide*,
Marx & Engels *Manifesto*, Spencer *Principles*, Simmel *Philosophy of Money*, Pareto *Mind and Society*,
Du Bois *Souls* + *Essays*). Large classical-sociology queue still in `raw/` root (remaining Durkheim, Weber,
Sumner, Cooley, Mead, Marx/Engels remainder). The full wish-list roadmap lives in
`Outstanding sources.md`; this file tracks what is actually acquired, queued, and ingested.

---

## How to use

- **Tier 1** — core scaffolding sources (discipline overviews, landmark studies,
  key theoretical monographs). Ingest first; they unlock the densest link graph.
- **Tier 2** — high-value follow-ons (restudies, method classics, regional
  syntheses, major handbooks).
- **Tier 3** — depth and coverage fill (specialist monographs, excavation
  reports, contemporary research fronts).
- Mark ingested items with ✅ and the ingest date; leave notes on what the
  source covered and what it left thin.

Sources in the un-ingested queue live in `raw/` root. After ingest, file into
discipline- or era-grouped subfolders under `raw/`.

---

Classical-sociology foundations. Most are already acquired and sitting in `raw/` root;
ingest roughly in the order below (founders first, so later pages have link targets).

## Queue notes


- Collection is new; bias unknown until audited.
- Prefer primary studies and peer-reviewed handbooks over textbooks for
  contested claims (textbooks lag the research front).
- Polemics / advocacy works: artifact-mode ingest only (see `CLAUDE.md`
  Source-Type Handling).
